# Appendix B: What Remains Open


**What Remains Open**

---

**Note added February 2026 — Triadic B-V-D Reading Closes One Hard Open Problem**

Analysis of the Hermetic observational record (see [Part XVIII](19_part_xviii.md)) identifies that Axiom Zero is more fully read as a *three co-equal mode* structure:

Current reading: B + V = D (bubble and void generate displacement as a conserved sum)

Fuller reading: ΔB + ΔV + ΔD = 0 (bubble, void, and displacement are three co-equal modes of one creation event)

**Consequence for the open problems:**

**Koide parameter θ = 0.222 rad — CLOSED as independent problem.**

θ is α expressed as an angle in the three-dimensional B-V-D modal space of foam excitations. It is not a separate problem. It is the same problem stated in a different geometric language. When α is derived from the D-mode closure condition, θ is simultaneously derived. With Part XXIII deriving the leading-order formula α⁻¹ = 8π^(5/2) × 47/48, θ is now geometrically grounded. The three hard open problems reduce to one.

**Fine structure constant α** — DERIVED (Part XXIII, February 2026, revised March 2026). The exact two-term formula α⁻¹ = 8π^{5/2} × [(|G|−1)/|G| + (V−F)/(d·|G|³)] = 137.035995, matching observation to 0.030 ppm with zero free parameters. All factors derived from foam cell geometry and Axiom Zero. Not a truncated series — exact and closed.

**Covariant vacuum density** remains open but is now precisely specified: the mathematical object is the local spectral density of the Dirac operator (identified via the Book of Thæ synthesis), decomposed into positive spectrum (B-density), negative spectrum (V-density), and spectral flow (D-density). This is the sole remaining hard open problem. It unlocks: dark energy equation of state, running coupling constants, Klein-Gordon from substrate dynamics, and W/Z masses.

The three hard open problems (α, θ, covariant density) are now one: covariant vacuum density. The mathematical target is defined.

---

**1. Fine Structure Constant α [CLOSED — Part XXIII, revised March 2026]**

α ≈ 1/137.036 is the electromagnetic coupling constant. Part XXIII derives the exact closed-form expression:

**Primary form (additive):** α⁻¹ = 8π^{5/2} × [(|G|−1)/|G| + (V−F)/(d·|G|³)]

**Equivalent (product):** α⁻¹ = 8π^{5/2} × [(|G|−1)/|G|] × [1 + (V−F)/(d·|G|²·(|G|−1))]

where |G| = 48 (order of Oh), V − F = 10 = |G|/(2|Stab|) − χ (group theory + topology), d = 3. These forms are algebraically identical — the formula is an exact two-term sum, not a truncated series. No higher-order corrections exist. Result: α⁻¹ = 137.035995 (0.03 ppm).

The expression has two contributions beyond the phase-space volume 8π^{5/2}:
(i) (|G|−1)/|G| = 47/48 = Axiom Zero exclusion of self-coupling. DERIVED.
(ii) (V−F)/(d·|G|³) = 10/331776 = boundary self-energy correction. DERIVED. The numerator (V−F = 10) from orbit-stabiliser + Plateau + Euler. The denominator (d·|G|³) from three identified factors: identity-channel weight |⟨e|A₁g⟩|² = 1/|G| (trivial rep normalisation in regular rep), coupling squared 1/|G|² (out-and-back amplitude), and directional average 1/d.

**Status: Derived. Exact closed form. All factors identified and derived from geometry + Axiom Zero. Zero free parameters. Discrepancy: 0.030 ppm. One formal step outstanding: explicit construction of boundary coupling operator in the regular representation of Oh to verify the identity-channel weight matrix element. This is a well-defined exercise in finite group representation theory, not a conceptual gap.**

**Downstream items now unblocked:** Bohr radius from foam parameters (Part XXIV), gate frequency absolute values, Koide parameter geometrically derived, Howard 40.5 Hz base frequency.

**2. Covariant Derivation of Vacuum Density [Collaborator Required — Target Specified]**

rho_vac(r) = rho_0 × (1 - 2GM/rc²) is consistent with the Schwarzschild metric but not derived from a covariant quantum field theory in curved spacetime. This is the primary gap between the decoherence paper and journal publication.

Under the triadic B-V-D reading, the vacuum density is a three-component coupled field — B-density, V-density, and D-density at each point in curved spacetime — not a single scalar. This specifies the tensor structure.

**Mathematical target (from Book of Thæ synthesis):** The covariant object is the local spectral density of the Dirac operator:

    ρ_μν(x) = ∫ λ dN_x(λ) · g_μν

where N_x(λ) is the local eigenvalue counting function. The three UFFT modes map as: B-density = positive Dirac spectrum, V-density = negative Dirac spectrum, D-density = spectral flow between them under metric variation. Covariance is automatic (the Dirac operator transforms correctly under diffeomorphisms). The UFFT ansatz ρ₀(1 − 2GM/rc²) is the weak-field approximation to this general construction evaluated in the Schwarzschild metric.

**Collaborator specification:** Compute the spectrum of the Dirac operator on a Schwarzschild background, verify that the local spectral density reproduces ρ₀(1 − 2GM/rc²) in the weak-field limit, and extract the strong-field corrections. This is established QFT-in-curved-spacetime methodology with a specific target.

**Downstream items blocked on covariant vacuum density:** Dark energy equation of state precision (closing the 18% residual in Part XXI), decoherence prediction full precision, Klein-Gordon equation from foam substrate dynamics, running coupling constants / beta functions, strong force string tension lattice QFT derivation, W/Z mass coupling derivation.

× l³ = rho_0 × l_P³ = m_P = const. Total lensing angle: 4GM/(c²b). GR
result confirmed from foam two-component model.

**6. Schrödinger Equation from Foam Dynamics [SUBSTANTIALLY CLOSED]**

CLOSED February 2026. The free-particle Schrödinger equation is the
non-relativistic limit of the Klein-Gordon equation --- the foam
relativistic wave equation. Procedure: (1) Klein-Gordon (∂²/∂t² - c²∇² +
(m_ec²/ħ)²)ψ = 0 is the foam wave equation for a massive particle. (2)
Factor out rest energy: ψ = φ × exp(-im_ec²t/ħ). (3) Non-relativistic
limit (∂²φ/∂t² << m_ec²/ħ × ∂φ/∂t, valid when v << c) yields iħ
∂φ/∂t = -ħ²/(2m_e) ∇²φ. (4) Adding foam pressure gradient potential
V(r): iħ ∂φ/∂t = [-ħ²/(2m_e) ∇² + V(r)] φ. Born rule derivation:
|ψ|² = probability is the foam wave intensity rule --- intensity =
amplitude² is the standard result for any wave interference pattern. It
is not a separate postulate of quantum mechanics; it is a direct
consequence of treating ψ as a foam wave amplitude. Remaining gap:
derive Klein-Gordon from foam substrate dynamics (requires covariant
vacuum density --- still open).

**7. Strong and Weak Forces [MECHANISM ESTABLISHED]**

Strong force: foam torsion around 3 independent lattice axes. Each axis
corresponds to one colour charge (r=x, g=y, b=z). Colour neutrality
(r+g+b=white) follows from torsion closure condition: theta_r +
theta_g + theta_b = 0 mod 2π. 8 gluons = 8 independent torsion
generators (3×3 hermitian traceless matrices, i.e., Gell-Mann matrices).
Confinement: torsion potential V(θ) = k(1-cosθ) plateaus at θ=π giving
constant force (string tension). Asymptotic freedom: same potential is
harmonic at θ→0 (short range), so coupling → 0. String tension σ =
k_torsion/l_P; numerically k_torsion ≈ 5 × α_strong × E_P ×
(l_P/r_proton)². Full lattice QFT derivation of string tension: blocked on covariant vacuum density.
Weak force: each foam discharge event creates a right-handed helical
topological structure. Left-handed fermion vortices (circulation
opposing motion) couple to this complementary right-handed discharge ---
they interact. Right-handed vortices (aligned) do not couple --- maximal
parity violation follows geometrically, not postulated. W± =
torsion-discharge states also coupled to EM longitudinal foam. Z⁰ = pure
torsion-discharge, no EM coupling. W/Z masses: blocked on covariant vacuum density.

**Independent confirmation (NCG):** The gauge group SU(3) × SU(2) × U(1) is also derived in the Connes noncommutative geometry programme from the finite spectral triple algebra A_F = ℂ ⊕ ℍ ⊕ M₃(ℂ) on a 4D spin manifold with KO-dimension 6. The three summands of A_F correspond exactly to the three gauge factors. The Higgs doublet emerges as the off-diagonal inner fluctuation between the ℍ and M₃(ℂ) summands. This is a mathematical theorem (Chamseddine-Connes-Marcolli, 2007), not a UFFT result, but it independently confirms that the SM gauge group is the unique gauge structure compatible with a 4D discrete substrate — consistent with UFFT's foam torsion derivation. See Book of Thæ synthesis (§3.1) for the full dictionary.

**8. Dark Matter and Dark Energy [SUBSTANTIALLY CLOSED]**

The Gauge Decoupling Theorem (Part XXII, Section 3) proves that surface modes carry no U(1), SU(3), or SU(2) charge — three independent geometric proofs, one per gauge group. Surface modes couple to gravity via the equivalence principle. Equipartition is derived from foam properties: quadratic Hamiltonian (Taylor expansion around Kelvin equilibrium), thermal contact (shared cell walls), and equilibrium distribution (Part XIX microstate statistics). The dark matter ratio is the isoperimetric ratio of the equilibrium foam cell:

Ω_DM/Ω_b = (6 + 12√3) / (8√2)^{2/3} = 5.315

Observed (Planck 2018): 5.364 ± 0.09. Match within 0.92%, zero free parameters. Result is robust across all plausible foam cell geometries (flat truncated octahedron: 5.315, curved Kelvin cell: 5.306, Weaire-Phelan: 5.288 — all within 1σ of observation). The old coordination-number × coupling-fraction formula (Ω_DM/Ω_b = coordination × coupling) is superseded.

Observed: 5.88 × 10⁻²⁷ kg/m³. Match within 18%, zero free parameters. The cosmological constant problem is dissolved: the ratio 10⁻¹²³ is (l_P/R_U)² — geometry, not fine-tuning. Remaining: exact equation of state (w ≈ −1, requires covariant vacuum density for precision). See Part XXI for full derivation.

**Complete cosmological density budget:** Baryonic matter (volume energy, gauge-coupled), dark matter (surface energy, gauge-decoupled), dark energy (pressure wave residual). All three derived from foam properties with zero free parameters.

**9. Double Slit Visibility Equation [CLOSED]**

→ 1 (no which-path). Complementarity: V² + D² ≤ 1 reproduced from foam

**11. Void Coupling Efficiency [SCALING LAW DERIVED]**

Coupling efficiency scaling law: η ≈ (l_P/λ)⁴ × Q² × exp(−P_Blake/ΔP),

amplitude. This gives the correct order of magnitude for SBSL
(~10⁻¹¹⁴). Key engineering implication: three-cone coherent geometry vs
single transducer --- Q improvement ~100×, giving Q² improvement of
~10⁴×. The cone geometry improvement prediction (~30× from acoustic
levitation analysis) is a LOWER BOUND; void coupling improves by ~10⁴×.
Absolute prefactor requires covariant QFT treatment --- open.

× exp(−P_Blake/ΔP). For sustained cavitation with multi-frequency

geometry. Direction is confirmed. Absolute magnitude requires the
